CSI Node Plugin Client** (`pkg/volume/csi/`):\\n- `csi_client.go`: The core CSI node plugin client implementing the `csiDriverClient` interface with methods like `NodePublishVolume`, `NodeStageVolume`, `NodeUnpublishVolume`, `NodeUnstageVolume`, and `NodeExpandVolume`. It is the main entry point (`ProbeVolumePlugins`) and registers the CSI plugin with the volume plugin manager. It creates Attachers, Detachers, Mounters, and Unmounters.\\n- `csi_attacher.go`: Implements `volume.Attacher` and `volume.Detacher` via `csiAttacher`. Uses Kubernetes VolumeAttachment objects and waits for attach/detach completion with lister-based polling.\\n- `csi_mounter.go`: Implements `volume.Mounter` and `volume.Unmounter` via `csiMountMgr`. Handles NodeStageVolume and NodePublishVolume.\\n- `csi_block.go`: Implements block volume mapper/unmapper (`csiBlockMapper`) for raw block volumes.\\n- `csi_drivers_store.go`: In-memory store for CSI driver information.\\n- `csi_metrics.go`: CSI volume metrics collection.\\n- `csi_util.go`: Utility functions for CSI volume operations.\\n- `expander.go`: CSI volume expansion support.\\n- `nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go`: Manages CSINode objects on behalf of the kubelet, keeping node topology and driver information up to date.\\n- `fake/fake_client.go`: Fake CSI client for testing.\\n- `fake/fake_closer.go`: Fake closer for testing.\\n- `testing/testing.go`: Test helpers for CSI volume tests.\\n\\n**2. CSI Node Plugin Client** (`pkg/volume/csi/`):\\n- `csi_client.go`: The core CSI node plugin client implementing the `csiDriverClient` interface with methods like `NodePublishVolume`, `NodeStageVolume`, `NodeUnpublishVolume`, `NodeUnstageVolume`, and `NodeExpandVolume`. This is the gRPC client that communicates with the CSI driver over a Unix socket.\\n- `csi_plugin.go`: The in-tree CSI volume plugin (`csiPlugin`) that implements `volume.VolumePlugin`. It is the main entry point (`ProbeVolumePlugins`) and registers the CSI plugin with the volume plugin manager. It creates Attachers, Detachers, Mounters, and Unmounters.\\n- `csi_attacher.go`: Implements `volume.Attacher` and `volume.Detacher` via `csiAttacher`. Uses Kubernetes VolumeAttachment objects and waits for attach/detach completion with lister-based polling.\\n- `csi_mounter.go`: Implements `volume.Mounter` and `volume.Unmounter` via `csiMountMgr`. Handles NodeStageVolume and NodePublishVolume gRPC calls.\\n- `csi_block.go`: Implements block volume mapper/unmapper (`csiBlockMapper`) for raw block volumes.\\n- `csi_drivers_store.go`: In-memory store for CSI driver information.\\n- `csi_metrics.go`: CSI volume metrics collection.\\n- `csi_util.go`: Utility functions for CSI volume operations.\\n- `expander.go`: CSI volume expansion support.\\n- `nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go`: Manages CSINode objects on behalf of the kubelet, keeping node topology and driver information up to date.\\n- `fake/fake_client.go`: Fake CSI client for testing, implementing all node and controller gRPC methods.\\n- `fake/fake_closer.go`: Fake closer for testing.\\n- `testing/testing.go`: Test helpers for CSI volume tests.\\n\\n**2. CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller** (`pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/`):\\n- `attach_detach_controller.go`: The main AttachDetach controller that watches pods and nodes, creates/deletes VolumeAttachment objects, and drives CSI attach/detach operations via the volume plugin framework.\\n- `reconciler/reconciler.go`: Reconciliation loop that compares desired vs actual state of volume attachments and triggers attach/detach operations.\\n- `cache/actual_state_of_world.go`: Tracks the actual state of attached/detached volumes.\\n- `cache/desired_state_of_world.go`: Tracks the desired state based on pod scheduling.\\n- `statusupdater/node_status_updater.go`: Updates node status with volume attachment information.\\n- `populator/desired_state_of_world_populator.go`: Populates the desired state of world from pod specs.\\n- `util/util.go`: Utility functions for the attach/detach controller.\\n\\n**3. CSI Volume Provisioner & PersistentVolume Controller** (`pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/`):\\n- `pv_controller.go`: The main PersistentVolume controller that handles volume binding, provisioning (via StorageClass provisioner field), and reclamation. It bridges CSI operations to the core storage API by invoking the volume plugin framework which routes to the CSI plugin.\\n- `pv_controller_base.go`: Base controller setup, informers, and event handling for the PV controller.\\n- `volume_host.go`: Implements the `volume.VolumeHost` interface for the PV controller context, giving CSI plugins access to Kubernetes API resources.\\n- `index.go`: PV index for efficient binding lookups.\\n\\n**4. CSI Migration** (`pkg/volume/csimigration/`):\\n- `plugin_manager.go`: Manages in-tree to CSI plugin migration, translating in-tree volume plugin operations to equivalent CSI operations using the csi-translation-lib.\\n\\nThe integration flow: Pods request PVCs → PV controller provisions/binds PVs (routing to CSI plugin) → AttachDetach controller creates VolumeAttachments via `csiAttacher` → Kubelet uses `csiDriverClient` (csi_client.go) to stage/publish volumes on the node via gRPC calls to the CSI driver socket.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
